***окаянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окаянный.html>окая́нный</a> (13586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Has the form of a past passive participle of the dated verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ока́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but with shifted stress.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаянный.html>окая́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okajánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> damned, cursed</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каяться.html>ка́яться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kájatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покаяться.html>пока́яться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokájatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:океанский.html>океа́нский</a> (10210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:океан.html>океа́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okeán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:океанский.html>океа́нский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okeánskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ocean, oceanic</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">окид-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okid-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оклеить.html>окле́ить</a> (20404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеить.html>кле́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kléitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окликать.html>оклика́ть</a> (16442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окликнуть.html>окли́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oklíknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно</a> (217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*okъno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oknó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>о́кна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>о́кон</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>window

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:око.html>о́к</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но́</a></b>

***око.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>око</a> (4603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oko</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃ekʷ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:око.html>о́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́чи</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:око.html>оче́й</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* <i><b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́чи</a></span></b></i> is actually an old nominative dual form for neuter nouns.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or poetic or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eye (used in proverbs and expressions)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́чи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрные</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>óči</b> čórnyje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dark eyes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́б</a> неймёт.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vídit <b>óko</b>, da zúb nejmjót.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>The eye</b> sees (it) but the tooth cannot take it.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ок-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — околевать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-кол-</b>; суффикс: <b>-е</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***околица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:околица.html>око́лица</a> (15618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:околица.html>око́лица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okólica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:околица.html>око́лицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:околица.html>око́лицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:околица.html>око́лиц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> village fence, village gate

<li>outskirts
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:околица.html>око́лицу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na vsju okólicu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">throughout the whole neighbourhood</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
